04126 
04142 arm_status arm_dct4_init_f32(
04143   arm_dct4_instance_f32 * S,
04144   arm_rfft_instance_f32 * S_RFFT,
04145   arm_cfft_radix4_instance_f32 * S_CFFT,
04146   uint16_t N,
04147   uint16_t Nby2,
04148   float32_t normalize)
04149 {
04150   /*  Initialize the default arm status */
04151   arm_status status = ARM_MATH_SUCCESS;
04152 
04153   /* Initializing the pointer array with the weight table base addresses of different lengths */
04154   float32_t *twiddlePtr[3] =
04155     { (float32_t *) Weights_128, (float32_t *) Weights_512,
04156     (float32_t *) Weights_2048
04157   };
04158 
04159   /* Initializing the pointer array with the cos factor table base addresses of different lengths */
04160   float32_t *pCosFactor[3] =
04161     { (float32_t *) cos_factors_128, (float32_t *) cos_factors_512,
04162     (float32_t *) cos_factors_2048
04163   };
04164 
04165   /* Initialize the DCT4 length */
04166   S->N = N;
04167 
04168   /* Initialize the half of DCT4 length */
04169   S->Nby2 = Nby2;
04170 
04171   /* Initialize the DCT4 Normalizing factor */
04172   S->normalize = normalize;
04173 
04174   /* Initialize Real FFT Instance */
04175   S->pRfft = S_RFFT;
04176 
04177   /* Initialize Complex FFT Instance */
04178   S->pCfft = S_CFFT;
04179 
04180   switch (N)
04181   {
04182     /* Initialize the table modifier values */
04183   case 2048u:
04184     S->pTwiddle = twiddlePtr[2];
04185     S->pCosFactor = pCosFactor[2];
04186     break;
04187   case 512u:
04188     S->pTwiddle = twiddlePtr[1];
04189     S->pCosFactor = pCosFactor[1];
04190     break;
04191   case 128u:
04192     S->pTwiddle = twiddlePtr[0];
04193     S->pCosFactor = pCosFactor[0];
04194     break;
04195   default:
04196     status = ARM_MATH_ARGUMENT_ERROR;
04197   }
04198 
04199   /* Initialize the RFFT/RIFFT */
04200   arm_rfft_init_f32(S->pRfft, S->pCfft, S->N, 0u, 1u);
04201 
04202   /* return the status of DCT4 Init function */
04203   return (status);
04204 }
